SELECT TOP #   obj.run, obj.camCol, str(obj.field, #) as field,  str(obj.rowc, #, #) as rowc, str(obj.colc, #, #) as colc,  str(dbo.fObj(obj.objId), #) as id,   str(obj.psfMag_g - #*obj.extinction_g, #, #) as g,  str(obj.psfMag_r - #*obj.extinction_r, #, #) as r,  str(obj.psfMag_i - #*obj.extinction_i, #, #) as i,  str(obj.psfMag_z - #*obj.extinction_z, #, #) as z,  str(#*distance, #, #) as D,  dbo.fField(neighborObjId) as nfield,  str(dbo.fObj(neighborObjId), #) as nid FROM  (SELECT obj.objId,  run, camCol, field, rowc, colc,  psfMag_u, extinction_u,  psfMag_g, extinction_g,  psfMag_r, extinction_r,  psfMag_i, extinction_i,  psfMag_z, extinction_z,  NN.neighborObjId, NN.distance  FROM PhotoObj as obj  JOIN neighbors as NN on obj.objId = NN.objId  WHERE  #*NN.distance between # and # and  NN.mode = # and NN.neighborMode = # and  run = # and camCol = # and  obj.type = # and (obj.flags & #) = # and  nchild = # and obj.psfMag_i < # and  (g - r between # and # and r - i between # and #)  ) as obj  JOIN PhotoObj as nobj on nobj.objId = obj.neighborObjId  WHERE   nobj.run = obj.run and  (abs(obj.psfMag_g - nobj.psfMag_g) < # or  abs(obj.psfMag_r - nobj.psfMag_r) < # or  abs(obj.psfMag_i - nobj.psfMag_i) < #)

SELECT TOP #   p.objid AS CATID,   p.ra AS RA,   p.dec AS DEC,    (sqrt(abs(power(p.petroR5#_r, #)/p.expAB_r - #*power(psffwhm_r, #)))   ) AS Re, -- convert circularised r_e to elliptical, for comparison with GAMA (Kelvin+#). abs() to avoid floating point error for unresolved sources.   s.z AS z,   (# + #*(p.ModelMag_g - p.ModelMag_i) -- ModelMag uses consistent (r-band) aperture     - #*(p.cModelMag_i - #*(log1#(s.z*#/#/#) + #))    ) as Mstar, -- stellar mass from (g-i) colour and i mag (Taylor+#)   p.cModelMag_u AS GAL_MAG_U, -- cModelMag is sum of deVaucouleurs + exponential profiles (https://www.sdss.org/dr1#/algorithms/magnitudes/)   p.cModelMag_g AS GAL_MAG_G,   p.cModelMag_r AS GAL_MAG_R,   p.cModelMag_i AS GAL_MAG_I,   p.petroMag_r + #*log1#(#*power(p.petroR5#_r, #)) AS GAL_RE_R, -- surface brightness within #re   (#-p.expAB_r) AS Ellipticity_r,   p.fracDeV_r AS fracDeV_r -- in the absence of sersic index, fractional contribution of deVaucouleurs profile to cModelMag FROM PhotoObj AS p   JOIN SpecObj AS s ON s.bestobjid = p.objid WHERE    ((p.type = #) -- galaxy     AND (p.dec BETWEEN # AND #) -- Stripe #     AND (p.ra BETWEEN # AND #) -- Stripe #     AND (s.z > #)   )
SELECT sp.ra,sp.dec,sp.z, sp.modelMag_u, sp.modelMag_g,sp.modelMag_r,sp.modelMag_i,sp.modelMag_z,PZ.objId,PZ.z,PZ.zErr,P.ra, P.dec,N.distance, P.u,P.g,P.r,P.i,P.z,PZ.synthU, PZ.synthG, PZ.synthR,PZ.synthI,PZ.synthZ,PZ.absMagU,PZ.absMagG,PZ.absMagR,PZ.absMagI,PZ.absMagZ into mydb.qsoxgal1# from SpecPhoto AS sp,      Photoz as PZ,      Neighbors  as N,      PhotoObj  AS P  WHERE sp.class = &&&    AND sp.zWarning = #    and sp.z > #    and sp.z < #	    and sp.modelMag_u<#    and PZ.z BETWEEN # and #    and PZ.nnCount># 	    and PZ.zErr BETWEEN # and #   and sp.z<((#+PZ.z+#)*#/#)#   and PZ.z<sp.z-#     and PZ.ObjID = N.ObjID		     and sp.ObjID = N.NeighborObjID  	     and N.distance < #/#     and PZ.ObjID =P.ObjID     and P.r>#     and P.r<#
SELECT    p.objid AS CATID,   p.ra AS RA,   p.dec AS DEC,    (sqrt(abs(power(p.petroR5#_r, #)/p.expAB_r - #*power(psffwhm_r, #)))   ) AS Re,    s.z AS z,   (# + #*(p.ModelMag_g - p.ModelMag_i)      - #*(p.cModelMag_i - #*(log1#(s.z*#/#/#) + #))   ) as Mstar,    p.cModelMag_u AS GAL_MAG_U,    p.cModelMag_g AS GAL_MAG_G,   p.cModelMag_r AS GAL_MAG_R,   p.cModelMag_i AS GAL_MAG_I,   p.petroMag_r + #*log1#(#*power(p.petroR5#_r, #)) AS GAL_RE_R,    (#-p.expAB_r) AS Ellipticity_r,   p.fracDeV_r AS fracDeV_r into mydb.MyTable from PhotoObj AS p   JOIN SpecObj AS s ON s.bestobjid = p.objid    WHERE    ((p.type = #)                AND (p.dec BETWEEN # AND #)      AND (p.ra BETWEEN # AND #)      AND (s.z > #)   )

SELECT TOP #   p.objid AS CATID,   p.ra AS RA,   p.dec AS DEC,    (sqrt(power(p.petroR5#_r, #)/p.expAB_r - #*power(psffwhm_r, #))   ) AS Re, -- convert circularised r_e to elliptical, for comparison with GAMA (Kelvin+#)   s.z AS z,   (# + #*(p.ModelMag_g - p.ModelMag_i) -- ModelMag uses consistent aperture     - #*(p.cModelMag_i - #*(log1#(s.z*#/#/#) + #))   ) as Mstar, -- stellar mass from (g-i) colour and i mag (Taylor+#)   p.cModelMag_u AS GAL_MAG_U, -- cModelMag is sum of deVaucouleurs + exponential profiles (https://www.sdss.org/dr1#/algorithms/magnitudes/)   p.cModelMag_g AS GAL_MAG_G,   p.cModelMag_r AS GAL_MAG_R,   p.cModelMag_i AS GAL_MAG_I,   -- surface brightnesses?   p.petroR5#_r + #*log1#(pi*power(p.petroR5#_r, #)) AS GAL_RE_R, -- surface brightness within #re   (#-p.expAB_r) AS Ellipticity_r,   p.fracDeV_r AS fracDeV_r -- in the absence of sersic index, fractional contribution of deVaucouleurs profile to cModelMag   -- or likelihood of deVaucouleurs profile (https://www.sdss.org/dr1#/algorithms/classify/) FROM PhotoObj AS p   JOIN SpecObj AS s ON s.bestobjid = p.objid   -- JOIN PhotoProfile AS pp ON pp.objid = p.objid -- for radial surface brightness profiles WHERE    ((p.type = #) -- galaxy     AND (p.b > # OR p.b < #)      AND (p.dec < #)     AND (s.z > #))

SELECT TOP #   p.objid AS CATID,   p.ra AS RA,   p.dec AS DEC,    (sqrt(power(p.petroR5#_r, #)/p.expAB_r - #*power(psffwhm_r, #))   ) AS Re, -- convert circularised r_e to elliptical, for comparison with GAMA (Kelvin+#)   s.z AS z,   (# + #*(p.ModelMag_g - p.ModelMag_i) -- ModelMag uses consistent aperture     - #*(p.cModelMag_i - #*(log1#(s.z*#/#/#) + #))   ) as Mstar, -- stellar mass from (g-i) colour and i mag (Taylor+#)   p.cModelMag_u AS GAL_MAG_U, -- cModelMag is sum of deVaucouleurs + exponential profiles (https://www.sdss.org/dr1#/algorithms/magnitudes/)   p.cModelMag_g AS GAL_MAG_G,   p.cModelMag_r AS GAL_MAG_R,   p.cModelMag_i AS GAL_MAG_I,   -- surface brightnesses?   p.petroR5# + #*log1#(pi*power(p.petroR5#, #)) AS GAL_RE_R, -- surface brightness within #re   pp.bin AS bin,   (#-p.expAB_r) AS Ellipticity_r,   p.fracDeV_r AS fracDeV_r -- in the absence of sersic index, fractional contribution of deVaucouleurs profile to cModelMag   -- or likelihood of deVaucouleurs profile (https://www.sdss.org/dr1#/algorithms/classify/) FROM PhotoObj AS p   JOIN SpecObj AS s ON s.bestobjid = p.objid   -- JOIN PhotoProfile AS pp ON pp.objid = p.objid -- for radial surface brightness profiles WHERE    ((p.type = #) -- galaxy     AND (p.b > # OR p.b < #)      AND (p.dec < #)     AND (s.z > #))
